## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: nonlinear dynamics / classical mechanics
**Analysis**: This task models the acceleration of a nonlinear harmonic oscillator, where dv_dt depends on position x (restoring force), velocity v (damping), and possibly time t (external driving). The nonlinearity can appear in the potential (anharmonic terms) or in the damping mechanism.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Linear oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x (simple harmonic restoring force)
- Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Duffing with quintic: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order anharmonic potential)
- Damped linear oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (restoring force with linear damping)
- Damped Duffing: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (Duffing with linear damping)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * x**2 * v (nonlinear damping proportional to x┬▓v)
- Driven oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * sin(c3 * t) (periodically driven damped oscillator)
- Driven Duffing: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (driven Duffing oscillator)
- Softening spring: dv_dt = c0 * x * (1 + c1 * x**2) (position-dependent spring constant)
- Pendulum-like: dv_dt = c0 * sin(c1 * x) (sinusoidal restoring force from pendulum dynamics)
- Cubic damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (nonlinear velocity-dependent damping)
- Rayleigh oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (Rayleigh-type nonlinear damping)
- Parametric oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x * (1 + c1 * cos(c2 * t)) (time-modulated spring constant)
- Coulomb + viscous damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v * (v**2 + c3)**(-0.5) (mixed damping model)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope тЖТ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects тЖТ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay тЖТ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior тЖТ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects тЖТ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, x┬│, xтБ╡) тЖТ symmetric potential wells preserving oscillator symmetry
- Terms like x┬▓*v or (1тИТx┬▓)*v тЖТ amplitude-dependent damping characteristic of self-excited oscillators (Van der Pol type)
- Sinusoidal time dependence sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) тЖТ external periodic driving force
- Product x*cos(c*t) тЖТ parametric excitation where the stiffness is modulated in time
- Absence of explicit time dependence тЖТ autonomous/conservative system; presence implies driven or parametric system
- Sign of velocity-dependent terms: negative c*v тЖТ energy dissipation; positive тЖТ energy injection (self-excitation)
- Rational powers of (x┬▓+v┬▓) тЖТ amplitude-dependent effects in polar/energy coordinates
- Mixed terms like x*v тЖТ velocity-position coupling indicating non-conservative or gyroscopic forces
